    var realtime = function(realtimeLoaded, msg){
        if(realtimeLoaded){
            return;
        }

        $.getScript('http://s.glbimg.com/bu/rt/js/glb-rt.js', function(){
            $.ajax({
                dataType: 'jsonp',
                
                url: 'http://s.glbimg.com/es/ge/static/live/globoesporte/json/globoesporte-home-agregador.js',
                
                jsonpCallback: 'glbrealtime_callback',
                cache: true,
                success: function(json){
                    $.glbrealtime({
                        data: json,
                        debug: false
                    });
                }
            });
        });
    }

    var realtimeLoaded = false;

    $(window).on('load', function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "onLoad");
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    })

    setTimeout(function(){
        realtime(realtimeLoaded, "timeout")
        realtimeLoaded = true;
    }, 3000);

  <script>
    $(document).ready(function(){
      var time = null,
          targetItem = $('.target-item');

      function hideShareIcons () {
        targetItem.fadeOut();
        $('.r7opened').removeClass('r7opened');
      }

      $('.open-item').hover(function() {
        var self = $(this);

        if(!self.hasClass('r7opened')){
          hideShareIcons();
        }
        clearTimeout(time);

        self.find('.target-item').stop(true, true).fadeIn("fast");
        self.addClass('r7opened');
      }, function(){
        time = setTimeout(hideShareIcons, 500);
      });

      var $searchBar = $('.header-menu-horizontal-search-bar'),
          $socialAndSearchHide = $('.header-menu-horizontal-social-items, .header-menu-horizontal-send-video'),
          $topVideoFilter = $searchBar.find('.r7-top-video-filter');

      $(document).on('click', function(e) {
        var t = $(e.target),
            mod = 'header-menu-horizontal',
            ignoredClasses = [mod + '-search-bar', mod + '-search', 'open-search-bar', 'search-icon', 'r7-top-video-main-form', 'r7-top-video-filter-opener', 'r7-top-video-input', 'r7-top-video-btn'],
            hasClass = true;

        _.each(ignoredClasses, function(item) {
          if(t.hasClass(item)) {
            hasClass = false;
          }
        });

        if (hasClass) {
          $searchBar.hide();
          $topVideoFilter.removeClass('is-visible');
          $socialAndSearchHide.removeClass('is-hidden').addClass('is-visible');
        }
      });

      $('.open-search-bar')
        .die('click')
        .on('click', function(e) {
          e.preventDefault();
          $searchBar.show();
          $socialAndSearchHide.addClass('is-hidden');
        });

      var checkInput = function() {
        var t = $(this), label = t.parent().find('label');

        if (t.val().length > 0) {
          label.fadeIn();
        }
        else {
          label.fadeOut();
        }
      };

      $('#login-input, #pass-input').on('focus blur keyup', checkInput);

      $('.search-action')
        .die('click')
        .on('click', function(e){
          return $('.header-menu-horizontal-search').val().length > 0;
        });

      var offset = $('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav').offset().top;

      $('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav').attr('data-offset', offset);

      var $window = $(window);

      $window.scroll(function(){
        var stickyShareTop = $('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav').attr('data-offset');
          scrollTop = $window.scrollTop();
          if (scrollTop > stickyShareTop) {
            $('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav:not(.sticky)').addClass('sticky');
            $('#header-menu-horizontal:not(.sticky)').addClass('sticky');
            $('.header-menu-horizontal-top-info:not(.bg-sticky)').addClass('sticky');
            $('.pre-main-content:not(.sticky)').addClass('bg-sticky');
          }
          else {
            if ($('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav').hasClass('sticky')){
              $('#header-menu-horizontal .header-menu-horizontal-nav').removeClass('sticky');
              $('#header-menu-horizontal').removeClass('sticky');
              $('.header-menu-horizontal-top-info').removeClass('sticky');
              $('.pre-main-content').removeClass('bg-sticky');
            }
          }
      });
    });
  </script>

          });

            if (conditional === 1) {
              return options.fn(this);

        }(SchumiBackbone.ServiceBox, Handlebars, Backbone, jQuery, _));

        <!-- Tracking -->
  <script type="text/javascript">
    // criando elemento para url canônica
    var linkCanonical   = document.createElement('link');
    linkCanonical.href  = "" || location.href;
    linkCanonical.rel   = "canonical";

    (function() {
      // adicionando metatag referente a url canonica dentro da tag <head/>
      document.head.appendChild(linkCanonical);

      //GOOGLE ANALYTICS UNIVERSAL 
      (function(i, s, o, g, r, a, m) {
          i['GoogleAnalyticsObject'] = r;
          i[r] = i[r] || function() {
              (i[r].q = i[r].q || []).push(arguments)
          }, i[r].l = 1 * new Date();
          a = s.createElement(o),
              m = s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];
          a.async = 1;
          a.src = g;
          m.parentNode.insertBefore(a, m)
      })(window, document, 'script', 'https://www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js', 'ga');

      ga('create', 'UA-10631407-1', 'auto');

      //evita ReferenceError
      dataLayer = (typeof dataLayer !== 'undefined')? dataLayer : {};
      if(dataLayer.page_name         ) {ga('set', 'dimension1',  dataLayer.page_name         );}
      if(dataLayer.site_section      ) {ga('set', 'dimension2',  dataLayer.site_section      );}
      if(dataLayer.sub_section       ) {ga('set', 'dimension3',  dataLayer.sub_section       );}
      if(dataLayer.sub_section_2     ) {ga('set', 'dimension4',  dataLayer.sub_section_2     );}
      if(dataLayer.sub_section_3     ) {ga('set', 'dimension5',  dataLayer.sub_section_3     );}
